     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>服务</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
     10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>”</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:
     Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>）。</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l43 level1 lfo1;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>相关服务在网站，微信小程序和应用程序上提供。</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>1.2</span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>条款何时适用并对用户具有约束力？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l17 level1 lfo2;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>本协议适用于任何人在安装、下载甚至仅仅访问或访问平台的任何部分或使用服务时，这些人被称为用户，包括但不限于浏览器用户、供应商、卖家和其他购买者或内容贡献者（统称为</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>“</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
     10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>”</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:
     Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>）。</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l17 level1 lfo2;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户与公司之间的协议在下载应用程序</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>访问网站之日和</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>或协议条款更新之日生效，在用户和公司之间建立具有法律约束力的安排。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>1.3 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>本协议条款是否可以修改？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l23 level1 lfo3;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户可以随时在网站上查看最新版本的协议。公司保留通过在平台上发布更新或更改来单方面更新、更改或替换本协议任何部分的权利，并且本协议的此类修改条款应在发布于平台后立即生效。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l23 level1 lfo3;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户有责任定期检查此页面的更改。用户在发布任何更改后继续使用或访问应用程序即表示接受这些更改。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>1.4 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>如果用户不接受本协议的条款怎么办？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l9 level1 lfo4;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>如果用户不同意本协议的条款，建议用户不要使用本平台。通过访问或使用平台，用户不可撤销地接受本协议并同意遵守本协议（不时更新）。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;

style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>账户注册、暂停和终止</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>2.1 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户是否一定需要在平台上创建账户？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo5;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户可以通过注册创建帐户来访问应用程序。用户资格仅限于购买或销售产品，受本协议约束，严格不得转让。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>2.2 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>对于平台的使用，用户是否符合任何资格标准？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l38 level1 lfo6;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>如果公司接到通知或公司发现用户不符合此处的条件，公司保留终止用户帐户和</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>或拒绝访问平台的权利。访问或使用平台的用户声明并保证他们有权访问或使用平台。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>2.3 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>在平台注册账号有什么具体要求吗？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l6 level1 lfo7;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户在平台注册时需要输入有效的电话号码。通过此类注册，用户同意公司通过电话、短信通知、即时消息或其他此类通信方式联系订阅</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>服务</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
     10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:
     Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>促销更新等。用户可以</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;
     line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'>“</span><span
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
     mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>选择退出</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'>”</span><span
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
     mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>此类订阅</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
     mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>服务</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
     mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>通过提供的</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'>“</span><span
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
     mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>退出</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'>”</span><span
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
     mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>方式或写信给支持团队的促销更新。</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;
     line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l6 level1 lfo7;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户有责任提供正确的手机号码，以便公司可以通过短信与用户进行通信。用户理解并同意，如因用户手机号码错误、数据不足或被用户服务提供商屏蔽等原因导致本公司发送短信而用户未收到，或用户因其他原因无法接收短信，公司应被视为有效地向用户提供了通信。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l6 level1 lfo7;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户有责任在注册过程中提供准确、最新和完整的信息，并更新此类信息以保持其准确、最新和完整。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>2.4 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>在平台上注册的用户账户可以被暂停或终止吗？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l35 level1 lfo8;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司保留暂停或终止应用程序上的帐户或访问服务（或其任何部分）的权利，包括冻结应付给用户和相关帐户的任何款项，恕不另行通知，并且用户将对截至和包括终止日期，如果：</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=I>
  <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
      191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l35 level2 lfo8;tab-stops:list 72.0pt;
      background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
      mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
      Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>在注册过程中或之后提供的任何信息被证明是不准确的、不是最新的或不完整的；和</span><span
      lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
      letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
      110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
      Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>或</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
      10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:
      .05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
  <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
      191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l35 level2 lfo8;tab-stops:list 72.0pt;
      background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
      mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
      Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>在公司的评估中，用户有：</span><span lang=EN-US
      style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
      letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
  <ul style='margin-top:0cm' type=square>
   <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
       191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l35 level3 lfo8;tab-stops:list 108.0pt;
       background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
       mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
       Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>收取不合理的高价；</span><span lang=EN-US
       style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
       letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
   <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
       191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l35 level3 lfo8;tab-stops:list 108.0pt;
       background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
       mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
       Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>发起不合理的退货和</span><span lang=EN-US
       style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
       letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
       110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
       Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>或取消事件；</span><span lang=EN-US
       style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
       letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
   <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
       191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l35 level3 lfo8;tab-stops:list 108.0pt;
       background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
       mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
       Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>从事欺诈、疏忽或损害公司利益的行为。</span><span lang=EN-US
       style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
       letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
   <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
       191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l35 level3 lfo8;tab-stops:list 108.0pt;
       background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
       mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
       Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>未能或被怀疑未能遵守本协议或适用法律的任何条款或规定。</span><span
       lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
       letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
  </ul>
  <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
      191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l35 level2 lfo8;tab-stops:list 72.0pt;
      background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
      mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
      Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>发现用户不遵守协议。</span><span lang=EN-US
      style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
      letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 </ol>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l35 level1 lfo8;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>此外，如果违反协议导致刑事或民事诉讼，公司可自行决定采取此类行动。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l35 level1 lfo8;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>在不损害公司上述权利的情况下，如果用户涉嫌欺诈或其他违反本协议的行为，公司可自行决定</span><span
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'> <span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>(a) </span><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>扣留所有应付给该用户的款项；</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>(b) </span><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>施加公司可合理确定的罚款，并从公司应支付给该用户的款项中抵消此类罚款。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>2.5 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户对其在平台上的注册账户有哪些义务？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l7 level1 lfo9;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>在平台上拥有一个帐户可以使用户的行为具有真实性。这意味着用户对其帐户下发生的所有活动负全部责任，并且该用户进行的所有交易均旨在善意销售或在业务活动过程中进行的消费。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l7 level1 lfo9;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户在其帐户下进行的任何和每一项活动均由该用户自行负责，并且公司对此类活动不承担任何责任。因此，作为安全程序的一部分，用户有责任将公司提供的用户识别码、密码和任何其他信息视为机密信息，并且不得将其透露给除公司之外的其他任何个人或实体。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l7 level1 lfo9;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户承认并同意，在平台上拥有账户并不授予其在平台上未由公司明确授予他们的任何权利，并且用户对该账户没有所有权或其他利益。用户理解，帐户中的所有权利以及应永远归公司所有，并符合公司的利益。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l7 level1 lfo9;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>注册时，用户可能会收到受密码保护的帐户和身份证明。用户同意：</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=I>
  <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
      191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l7 level2 lfo9;tab-stops:list 72.0pt;
      background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
      mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
      Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>维护其密码的机密性（如果适用）；</span><span lang=EN-US
      style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
      letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
  <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
      191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l7 level2 lfo9;tab-stops:list 72.0pt;
      background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
      mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
      Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>对用户通过其帐户访问应用程序的所有活动承担全部责任；</span><span
      lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
      letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
  <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
      191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l7 level2 lfo9;tab-stops:list 72.0pt;
      background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
      mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
      Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>立即通知公司对其帐户的任何未经授权的使用或他们意识到的任何其他违反安全性的行为；和</span><span
      lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
      letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
  <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
      191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l7 level2 lfo9;tab-stops:list 72.0pt;
      background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
      mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
      Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>确保他们在每次会话结束时退出帐户。</span><span lang=EN-US
      style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
      letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 </ol>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:72.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:72.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>3. </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>下订单和财务条款</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>3.1 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>如何在平台下订单？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l5 level1 lfo10;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>该应用程序允许用户为供应商在应用程序上列出的产品下订单，并且该应用程序在遵守此处协议的情况下有助于用户下订单产品。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l5 level1 lfo10;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>在收到用户的订单后，公司应以电子方式向供应商和相关用户发送该订单的确认。此外，公司可能会不时通知用户有关供应商告知的订单的可用性或不可用性或价格变化。供应商对订单的确认应视为最终决定。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l5 level1 lfo10;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司不自行拥有、销售或转售任何产品和</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>或不控制供应商，仅促进买家和卖家之间的交易，包括作为</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>“</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>市场</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
     10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>”</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:
     Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>的用户和供应商。公司尽一切合理努力及时更新用户帐户和其他信息，以协助促进交易完成。因此，用户必须为在应用程序上进行的所有购买提供当前、完整和准确的购买和帐户信息。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l5 level1 lfo10;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>此外，卖家对其最终用户</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>消费者的订单履行应由供应商与此类最终用户</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>消费者负责。平台为此类订单提供的任何附加服务应仅由平台作为该供应商的服务提供者提供，因此平台与该最终用户</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>消费者不具有任何合同关系。</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>3.2 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>应用程序中的商业条款是如何确定的？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l13 level1 lfo11;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>所有商业</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
     10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:
     Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>合同销售条款均由供应商提供，并由供应商和用户单独商定。商业</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>合同条款包括但不限于价格、日期、交付期限和方式、与产品相关的保证等。公司没有任何控制权，也不决定或建议或以任何方式参与提供或接受供应商与用户之间的此类商业</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>合同条款。所有佣金，折扣和优惠均由供应商而非公司提供。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l13 level1 lfo11;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>同样，在卖家使用平台进行交付的情况下，平台仅充当卖家的服务提供商，以促进交付或与订单相关的其他服务。公司没有任何控制权，也不会决定或建议或以任何方式参与卖家与其最终用户</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>消费者之间此类商业</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>合同条款的提供或接受。</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l13 level1 lfo11;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>与退货</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
     10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:
     Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>换货、罚款、退款、取消相关的政策将不时在应用程序中更新。本公司有权在未经用户许可的情况下根据应用程序中的要求更改这些政策。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>3.3 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>平台的支付和结算是如何运作的？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo12;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户承认并同意，公司可应供应商或卖家的要求，作为支付代理，以有限的目的代表此类供应商和卖家接受付款。用户理解、接受并同意公司提供的支付工具既不是银行服务也不是金融服务，而仅仅是为应用程序上的交易提供第三方支付处理器的促进者。此外，通过提供支付便利，公司既不作为受托人，也不以受托人的身份就交易或交易价格行事。本公司对用户银行就支付总金额所收取的任何费用概不负责。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo12;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>对于任何订单，可能需要向公司或第三方支付处理商提供姓名、账单地址和信用卡信息等信息。如果用户被定向到第三方支付处理器，他们可能会受到管理该第三方服务使用和该第三方个人信息收集做法的条款和条件的约束。请用户在使用应用程序之前查看此类条款和条件以及隐私政策。如果卖家向公司或其他交付服务提供商提供其最终用户</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>消费者的账单信息、送货地址或其他联系信息，则卖家应确保其获得相应最终用户</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>消费者的必要同意和批准，如可能要求适用法律。</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo12;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司仅代表供应商或卖家收取款项（视情况而定）。所有适用的税费、税率以及此类税费的适用方式均由供应商或卖家收取和确定。公司对征收此类税款的法律正确性</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>有效性不承担任何责任。与应付税款有关的任何法律问题的唯一责任应由供应商或卖家承担。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo12;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>交易是供应商和用户和</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>或卖家和最终用户</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>消费者之间的双边交易（</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>“</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户交易</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
     10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>”</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:
     Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>），公司不负责收取或缴纳任何适用于此类交易的税款。</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
     10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>3.4 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司是否就公司在平台上提供的服务向用户收费？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l15 level1 lfo13;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>平台上的服务可能需要支付费用，费用由公司自行决定，并须在用户在平台下订单时获得批准。公司保留随时自行决定修改服务收费的权利。在任何给定时间适用的费用将是用户在平台上购买</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>预订相应服务（如果有）时显示的费用。</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l15 level1 lfo13;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司保留在平台上引入额外收费服务的权利，包括溢价退货服务费、取消费、货到付款手续费等。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>3.5 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>在平台上进行交易是否需要用户根据中央或州商品和服务税立法（</span></b><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>“GST
</span></b><b><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>法律</span></b><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>”</span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>）进行注册？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l26 level1 lfo14;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司不承担因用户访问或使用平台服务而可能产生的用户任何直接或间接税收义务。根据</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'> GST </span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;
     line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;
     mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>法律和其他税法进行注册和遵守的要求是用户（包括卖家）的全部责任，对于此类用户违反任何适用法律的行为的任何遗漏或佣金，公司概不负责。因此，建议用户通过平台寻求与其业务和</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>或交易有关的独立税务建议，包括是否有责任注册</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'> GST</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>。</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
     10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span

mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>平台的使用</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>4.1 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户可以随时访问和使用平台吗？是否有任何限制？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:

     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司努力使应用程序</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'> 24X7 </span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;
     line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;
     mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>可用。但是，本公司并不表示对应用程序的访问将是不间断的、及时的、无错误的、无病毒或其他有害成分的，或者此类缺陷将得到纠正。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l29 level1 lfo15;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户理解并承认使用应用程序需要互联网连接和电信链接。用户应承担访问和使用应用程序和使用服务所产生的费用，并且公司在任何情况下均不对此类费用负责或承担责任。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l29 level1 lfo15;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司不保证应用程序将与用户使用的所有硬件和软件兼容。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l29 level1 lfo15;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>应用程序可能会不断升级，某些功能和特性可能无法完全运行。公司明确拒绝就其向用户提供的记录和其他数据提供任何形式的明示或暗示保证。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l29 level1 lfo15;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户应对其数据系统的损坏或因从应用程序下载内容而导致的数据丢失承担全部责任。除非另有说明，否则从公司或通过平台获得的任何书面或口头指导或信息均不构成任何保证。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;

style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司是否保证履行用户之间或其他有关平台产品的协议或其他安排？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:

     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司通过平台仅是交易的促进者，包括供应商和用户之间的交易，不对任何不履行或违反针对用户交易订立的任何合同负责。本公司不能也不保证相关供应商将执行在平台上达成的任何交易。本公司不应亦无义务调解或解决有关用户（包括与任何其他第三方）之间的任何争议或分歧。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l37 level1 lfo16;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>本公司不代表任何用户或供应商，并且对于平台上显示的与此类供应商或用户有关的任何信息的任何错误或不一致不承担任何责任。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l37 level1 lfo16;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>本公司不对任何用户的物品细节（如法定所有权、信誉、身份等）作出任何陈述或保证。公司不对任何滥用用户与其共享的信息的行为负责；或通过用户个人资料；或在平台、聊天室、论坛或评论上与第三方合作。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l37 level1 lfo16;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户承认并同意，本公司不是知识产权纠纷的仲裁员或法官，不能以任何方式验证任何在平台上</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>通过平台销售或供应商品的供</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>​​</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>应商或卖家是否有权销售产品。公司鼓励用户协助其识别平台上的列表，根据用户的知识或信仰侵犯其权利或第三方权利。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l37 level1 lfo16;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>在任何供应商和用户之间的任何交易期间，公司不会在任何时间点占有所提供的任何产品，也不会在任何时候获得对此类产品的所有权或任何权利或索赔。公司在任何时候均不对产品拥有任何权利、所有权或利益，也不对用户之间签订的此类合同承担任何义务或责任。公司不对因缺货、不可用或延期订购的产品造成的损坏或延误负责。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>4.3 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>平台（</span></b><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>a</span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>）的使用是否受到任何方式的限制；</span></b><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>(b) </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>要求用户遵守任何一般规定？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l25 level1 lfo17;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户不得使用平台托管、显示、上传、下载、修改、发布、传输、更新或共享以下任何信息：</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=I>
  <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
      191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l25 level2 lfo17;tab-stops:list 72.0pt;
      background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
      mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
      Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>严重有害、骚扰、亵渎、诽谤、淫秽、色情、恋童癖、诽谤、诽谤、犯罪煽动或侵犯他人隐私、仇恨或在种族、民族上令人反感、贬低、涉及或鼓励洗钱或赌博，或以其他方式非法任何方式；或非法威胁或非法骚扰。</span><span
      lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
      letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
  <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
      191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l25 level2 lfo17;tab-stops:list 72.0pt;
      background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
      mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
      Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>明显冒犯在线社区，例如色情内容，或宣扬针对任何团体或个人的淫秽、恋童癖、种族主义、偏执、仇恨或任何形式的身体伤害的内容；</span><span
