      Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
      .05pt'>所有适用的国内法律、规则和法规（包括任何适用的现行外汇管制法律或法规的规定）；</span><span lang=EN-US
      style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
      letter-spacing:.05pt'>(iii) </span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;
      line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;
      mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>关于应用程序的使用和上市、购买、招揽报价的国际法、外汇法、法令、条例和法规（包括但不限于根据该国现行法规适用的直接税和间接税）购买和销售产品或服务。用户不得从事任何适用法律规定禁止的任何交易，包括当时有效的外汇管制法律或法规。</span><span
      lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
      letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
  <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
      191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l25 level2 lfo17;tab-stops:list 72.0pt;
      background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
      mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
      Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>为了允许公司在不违反任何权利或任何法律的情况下使用用户提供的信息，用户同意授予公司非排他性的、全球性的、永久的、不可撤销的、免版税的、可分许可的（通过多层）行使版权、宣传、数据库权利或任何其他权利的权利。公司将仅根据本协议使用适用于平台使用和提供服务的信息。</span><span
      lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
      letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 </ol>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l25 level1 lfo17;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>如果任何用户未能遵守本协议的任何规定，公司应不时自行决定保留禁用任何用户识别码或密码的权利。公司有权采取必要的行动并要求赔偿可能因用户以任何方式自行或通过一群人有意或无意地参与黑客攻击而造成的损害。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>5. </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>平台信息的准确性和完整性</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>5.1 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>平台上显示的所有信息的准确性和完整性如何？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l8 level1 lfo18;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司尽最大努力保持平台上的信息准确无误。但是，平台上的材料和内容仅供一般参考，在未咨询主要、更准确、更完整或更及时的信息来源的情况下，不应依赖或用作决策的唯一依据。参考下文第</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'> 5.2 </span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;
     line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;
     mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>段，用户同意平台上展示的大部分内容（包括产品）由各自的供应商提供，供应商应始终负责提供与其列出的此类产品相关的信息。除了合理检查以确保平台的一般卫生外，公司不对此类内容或信息进行任何控制。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l8 level1 lfo18;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>除法律要求外，公司不承担更新、修改或澄清平台信息的义务，包括但不限于定价信息。公司对确保用户提供的信息的准确性不承担任何责任或义务。对平台材料的任何依赖均由用户自行承担风险。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l8 level1 lfo18;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>平台可能包含某些历史信息。历史信息必然不是最新的，仅供您参考。本公司保留随时修改平台内容的权利，但没有义务更新平台上的任何信息。用户全权负责监控平台信息的变化。不应采取适用于平台的指定更新或刷新日期来表明平台上或与服务有关的所有信息已被修改或更新。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l8 level1 lfo18;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>有时，平台上的信息可能包含印刷错误、不准确或遗漏，这些信息可能与与产品、定价、促销、优惠、运费、运输时间和可用性有关的信息有关。如果平台上的任何信息不准确，公司保留随时更正任何错误、不准确或遗漏以及更改或更新信息的权利，恕不另行通知。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l8 level1 lfo18;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>信息按</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
     10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>“</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:
     Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>原样</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'>”</span><span
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
     mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>提供，不保证完整性、准确性、及时性或使用信息所获得的结果，也没有任何明示或暗示的保证，包括但不限于性能保证，适销性和对特定目的的适用性。本协议中的任何内容均不得在任何程度上替代用户的独立调查以及合理的技术和商业判断。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>5.2 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>平台上的产品相关信息是否由公司提供？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l40 level1 lfo19;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>并非平台上的所有信息均由公司提供。作为供应商的用户会不时提供与他们拟出售的产品相关的信息，并因此对其负责。在这方面，供应商承诺所有此类信息在所有方面均准确无误。供应商不鼓励也不应夸大或过分强调此类产品的属性，以任何方式误导用户。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l40 level1 lfo19;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司保留对平台上发布的材料进行监控的权利，但没有义务。但是，公司有权删除或编辑其自行决定违反或涉嫌违反任何适用法律或本条款精神的任何内容。在任何情况下，公司均不对发布的任何内容或因使用平台上的内容和</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>或内容出现而导致的任何索赔、损害或损失承担任何责任或义务。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l40 level1 lfo19;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>供应商对有关拟在平台上出售或提议出售或购买的产品的具体细节（如质量、价值、可销售性等）的正确性承担全部责任。公司不暗示或明确支持或认可任何产品的销售或购买，也不对出售给用户的产品提供任何保证</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>保证，在任何情况下，此类产品均不属于公司的责任。公司不声明或保证平台上提供的信息是正确、准确或可靠的。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l40 level1 lfo19;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司不对任何用户（包括供应商）在应用程序上提供的任何不准确、不完整或过时的信息负责。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>6. </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>上市和销售</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>6.1 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>作为供应商，除本协议外，用户还需要遵守哪些其他条款？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l44 level1 lfo36;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>除本协议外，供应商还受适用法律的约束，包括但不限于以下法律：</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=I>
  <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
      191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l44 level2 lfo36;tab-stops:list 72.0pt;
      background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
      mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
      Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>法定计量（包装商品）规则（包装规则）；</span><span lang=EN-US
      style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
      letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
  <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
      191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l44 level2 lfo36;tab-stops:list 72.0pt;
      background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
      mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
      Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>药品和化妆品法；</span><span lang=EN-US
      style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
      letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
  <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
      191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l44 level2 lfo36;tab-stops:list 72.0pt;
      background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
      mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
      Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>食品安全和标准法，食品安全和标准（包装和标签）条例，食品安全和标准（食品标准和食品添加剂）条例，食品安全和标准（食品或保健品、营养保健品、特殊医学用途食品、功能性食品和新型食品）条例。</span><span
      lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
      letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 </ol>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l44 level1 lfo36;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>根据上述法规和本协会任期内的任何其他相关法律，公司理解供应商有义务确保销售产品的包装符合标签和包装要求以及其他法律可在这方面作出规定。因此，供应商应全权负责遵守适用的法律，公司不承担任何责任。供应商应赔偿公司和平台因违反上述规定或其他适用法律而造成的任何损害或损失。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>6.2 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>供应商什么时候可以列出他们的产品？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo37;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>允许供应商根据本协议中提及的条款以及为此目的与公司签订的其他合同在应用程序上列出待售产品，其中详细规定了各方的其他权利和义务。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo37;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>通过在平台上发布其产品，供应商声明并保证他们具有在平台上销售或发布产品的合法能力；所列项目不侵犯任何第三方的知识产权、商业秘密或其他专有权利或公开权或隐私权。供应商和用户同意，本公司对违反本协议的行为不承担任何责任。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p style='margin:0cm;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;
line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;
line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;color:#404040;mso-themecolor:
text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>7. </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户信息和第三方工具</span></b><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>链接</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>7.1 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>从用户那里收集哪些信息？公司如何处理用户在使用平台时向其提供的信息？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo38;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司收集各类信息，有些信息是非个人信息，有些是个人信息。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo38;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>在平台上以任何方式收集、存储或传输的有关用户的所有信息都经过处理，以促进平台上的各种操作，包括注册、下订单、列表或付款。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo38;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>为了更全面地了解，鼓励用户查看平台上提供的平台隐私政策。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>7.2 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司是否在平台上使用第三方工具？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l30 level1 lfo39;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司可能会通过平台向用户提供对第三方工具的访问权限，这些工具公司既没有监控也没有任何控制或输入。用户承认并同意，对此类工具的访问是在</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>“</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>原样</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
     10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>”</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:
     Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>和</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'>“</span><span
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
     mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>可用</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'>”</span><span
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
     mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>的基础上进行的，没有任何形式的保证、陈述或条件，也没有公司的任何认可。公司不承担因您使用可选的第三方工具而引起的或与之相关的任何责任。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l30 level1 lfo39;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户对通过应用程序</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>平台提供的可选工具的任何使用完全由其自行承担风险和自由裁量权，并且用户有责任确保其熟悉并批准由相关的第三方供应商。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l30 level1 lfo39;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司可能会不时通过平台提供新功能，其中可能包括使用新的第三方工具和资源。此类新功能也应受本协议约束。有关第三方工具或第三方网站的投诉、索赔、疑虑或问题应直接提交给第三方。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>7.3 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司是否在平台上使用第三方链接或第三方工具？这些链接和工具是否准确且安全？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l42 level1 lfo40;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>通过平台提供的某些内容或产品可能包括来自第三方的材料。应用程序</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>平台上的第三方链接可能会将用户引导至与公司无关的第三方网站。本公司不负责检查或评估内容或准确性，也不保证也不会对任何第三方材料或网站，或第三方的任何其他材料、产品或服务承担任何责任或义务。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l42 level1 lfo40;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>无论平台上是否存在任何第三方链接，公司对与购买或使用商品、服务、资源、内容或与任何第三方网站相关的任何其他交易相关的任何损害或损害概不负责。请仔细阅读此类第三方的政策和做法，并确保在进行任何交易之前了解它们。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>8. </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>知识产权</span></b><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>
(IP) </span></b><b><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>和知识产权侵权</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>8.1 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户在与其他方开展业务时，能否使用平台上发布的</span></b><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>“Shopji”</span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>标志等内容？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l11 level1 lfo25;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>未经第三方事先书面许可，用户不得使用任何独立第三方的商标、服务标志或标识。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l11 level1 lfo25;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'>“Shopji”</span><span
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
     mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>以及相关图标和徽标（无论是否注册）均为公司的商标，并受适用的版权、商标和其他专有和知识产权法律的保护。严禁用户未经授权复制、修改、使用或发布这些标志。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l11 level1 lfo25;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户不得以任何方式修改打印或下载的任何材料的纸质或数字副本，并且不得将任何插图、照片、视频或音频序列或任何图形与任何随附文本分开使用。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l11 level1 lfo25;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>未经公司许可，用户不得将平台上的任何部分材料用于商业目的。特此保留公司未在本协议项下另行主张的所有权利。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l11 level1 lfo25;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户了解平台和平台内包含的软件可能包括允许保护数字材料的安全组件，并且这些材料的使用受公司或其他促进相同的各方设置的使用规则的约束。用户同意不会试图覆盖、禁用、规避或以其他方式干扰平台中嵌入的任何此类安全组件和使用规则。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>8.2 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司如何处理知识产权侵权？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l34 level1 lfo26;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>任何用户或供应商的任何商标、文字标记或知识产权仅属于该用户</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>供应商，公司对此没有任何权利或主张。</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l34 level1 lfo26;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司保留自行决定删除平台上显示的任何材料</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>内容</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
     10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:
     Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>照片</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
     mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>优惠的权利，这些材料</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;
     line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
     mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>内容</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
     mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>照片</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
     mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:
     .05pt'>报价在公司合理认为是非法的或可能使公司承担责任或违反本协议或以其他方式被认为不适合公司的观点。公司保留配合这方面的任何调查的权利。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l34 level1 lfo26;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司保留在其认为适当的情况下暂停或终止用户帐户的权利。用户同意，如果公司根据知识产权侵权指控采取任何行动，公司对任何用户不承担任何责任，包括后果性或任何其他损害赔偿责任。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l34 level1 lfo26;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户承认并同意，公司不是知识产权纠纷的仲裁员或法官，不能以任何方式验证任何在平台上销售或供应商品的供</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>​​</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>应商是否有权销售产品。公司鼓励用户协助其识别平台上的列表，根据用户的知识或信仰侵犯其权利或第三方权利。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l34 level1 lfo26;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>将产品从平台下架是为了维护公司的利益，通过删除列表，公司不会也不能被视为认可侵权索赔，并且在公司拒绝删除列表的情况下，公司不会并且不能被视为认可该列表不侵犯第三方权利或认可根据或基于此类列表的任何商品或服务的销售或供应。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l34 level1 lfo26;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>我们要求您查看应用程序中提供的知识产权政策以获取更多信息。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>9. </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>免责声明和责任</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>9.1</span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>关于平台和服务的标准免责声明是什么？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l28 level1 lfo27;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>对于任何特殊、偶然、间接的合同、疏忽、严格责任或其他法律或衡平法理论，公司在任何情况下均不对用户（包括卖家或通过用户提出索赔的任何人）承担任何责任、后果性、惩戒性或惩罚性损害赔偿、商誉损失、收入损失、机会损失、预期利润损失，包括因使用、数据或利润损失而导致的损失，无论是否可预见或公司是否已经被告知此类损害的可能性，或基于任何责任理论，包括违反合同或保证或疏忽或因使用或访问平台而引起或与之相关的任何其他索赔。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l28 level1 lfo27;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司不承担任何责任：任何伤害、损失、索赔或任何直接、间接、偶然、惩罚性、特殊或后果性损害，包括但不限于任何财务损失、数据丢失、更换成本或任何类似的损害赔偿，无论是基于合同、侵权、严格责任或其他，因使用平台或以任何方式与使用应用程序相关的任何其他索赔，包括但不限于任何错误或遗漏因使用应用程序</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>平台或通过应用程序</span><span lang=EN-US
     style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>平台发布、传输或以其他方式提供的任何内容而产生的任何内容或任何类型的任何损失或损害，即使被告知其可能性。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l28 level1 lfo27;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>用户应对其数据系统的损坏（如有）或从平台下载内容而导致的数据丢失承担全部责任。除非另有说明，否则从公司或通过平台获得的任何书面或口头指导或信息均不构成任何保证。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ol>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:110%;background:white'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>9.2 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191'>关于平台上包含、分发或链接、下载或访问的广告（包括其下的任何信息或报价）（</span></b><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191'>“</span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191'>广告</span></b><b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191'>”</span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191'>）的免责声明是什么？</span></b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>9.3 </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>如果发生锁定或其他不可抗力事件，用户订单会怎样？</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ol style='margin-top:0cm' start=1 type=a>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:
     191;line-height:110%;mso-list:l18 level1 lfo28;tab-stops:list 36.0pt;
     background:white'><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;
     mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>对于因不可抗力或其他类似情况而直接或间接影响公司和</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:
     110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
     Arial;letter-spacing:.05pt'>或平台的任何损害，公司概不负责。不可抗力事件的示例包括但不限于实际或潜在的劳资纠纷、政府行为、战争或战争威胁、破坏、内乱、示威、火灾、风暴、洪水、爆炸、地震、流行病或流行病、材料的规定或限制或资源、无法获得相关授权、事故和电力或电信网络缺陷。</span><span
     lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
     letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></li>

color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>11. </span></b><b><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>适用于协议的其他条款</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>11.1
</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>本协议受交易所在国法律管辖。为解决本协议或平台引起或与之相关的任何事项而开始的任何诉讼、诉讼或其他法律程序均应受交易所在国法律管辖。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>11.2
</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司有权将其在本协议中的义务和义务转让给任何个人或实体。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>11.3
</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司未能行使或执行本协议的任何权利或规定不构成对该权利或规定的放弃。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:110%;background:white'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>11.4
</span><span style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:
Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>公司保留向平台引入和启动新特性、功能和组件和</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>/</span><span
style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;
mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#404040;
mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'>或更改、更改、修改、暂停、停止或删除现有特性、功能和组件的权利，恕不另行通知您。此外，公司有权终止（永久或暂时）提供的一项或多项服务，或终止平台或提前免费收取服务费用，而无需事先通知用户。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#404040;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-themetint:191;letter-spacing:.05pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
